Mastering Genetics - Submit zeros for students who did not start the assignment/Manage Incompletes

Name of agent: Christopher Bustamante

Team Leader: Frezalin Bascara

Team: T2

Category: Mastering - Gradebook

Questions/Comments/Notes to raise on CTS/Prod Support Call: We understand that this is FAD. This case originated from FS, where the FS team and FS Specialist explained to the EDU that students receive a score of zero due to the settings applied to the assignments, even though they have not completed them yet. Despite this explanation, the EDU insisted that there are some technical issues with the assignments or gradebook. As a result, the FS team decided to escalate the case to TS as the FS Specialist mentioned that they have seen similar case escalated to TS. From the Tier 2 side, we've reviewed the support site before I escalate the case, though I was not able to mention that the EDU needs to uncheck the box each time they manage incompletes and point out that the EDU has the option to delete the zero scores. But we were able to inform the EDU that this is working as designed. We also provided the support site - https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm to the instructor for review; however, the EDU continues to insist that there is something wrong with their gradebook and assignment settings that is why we decided to escalate the case for further review.

Case number: 50416963

INC number: INC0492379

Opened: 2024-09-06 21:22:32

Resolved: 2024-09-09 13:19:49

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Closed

FAD Reason: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

Revel - Total points not changing even after editing the Global settings

Name of agent: Floricel Blando

Team Leader: Frezalin Bascara

Team: T2

Category: Revel - Gradebook

Case number: 50467926

INC number: INC0495929

Opened: 2024-09-11 17:59:55

Assignment group: Revel Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD, Scoring_Policy

Assigned to: Jena Subrat

Resolution notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. Changing the Global Scoring policy only makes changes to items that have not been engaged by a student and locked. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

Name of agent: Rica Aiza Cruz

Team Leader: Ronald Villa

Team: T2

Category: XL - Gradebook

Case number: 50195850

INC number: INC0475294

Opened: 2024-08-21 10:49:53

Resolved: 2024-08-21 12:56:40

Assignment group: 3PL Product Escalation

Tags: 3PL_1.3, 3PL_FAD, 3PL_GS

Assigned to: Ben Lethlean

Resolution notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

Name of agent: Michael Pan

Team Leader: T3 TL

Category: Mastering - Assignment

Case number: 50558734

INC number: INC0500673

Opened: 2024-09-17 01:49:56

Resolved: 2024-09-17 04:17:09

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

Name of agent: Rica Aiza Cruz

Team Leader: Ronald Villa

Team: T2

Category: XL - Gradebook

Case number: 50195850

INC number: INC0475294

Opened: 2024-08-21 10:49:53

Resolved: 2024-08-21 12:56:40

Assignment group: 3PL Product Escalation

Tags: 3PL_1.3, 3PL_FAD, 3PL_GS

Assigned to: Ben Lethlean

Resolution notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

Name of agent: Michael Pan

Team Leader: T3 TL

Team: T3

Category: Mastering - Assignment

Case number: 50558734

INC number: INC0500673

Opened: 2024-09-17 01:49:56

Resolved: 2024-09-17 04:17:09

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Category: Mastering - Gradebook

Questions/Comments/Notes to raise on CTS/Prod Support Call: We understand that this is FAD. This case originated from FS, where the FS team and FS Specialist explained to the EDU that students receive a score of zero due to the settings applied to the assignments, even though they have not completed them yet. Despite this explanation, the EDU insisted that there are some technical issues with the assignments or gradebook. As a result, the FS team decided to escalate the case to TS as the FS Specialist mentioned that they have seen similar case escalated to TS. From the Tier 2 side, we've reviewed the support site before I escalate the case, though I was not able to mention that the EDU needs to uncheck the box each time they manage incompletes and point out that the EDU has the option to delete the zero scores. But we were able to inform the EDU that this is working as designed. We also provided the support site - https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm to the instructor for review; however, the EDU continues to insist that there is something wrong with their gradebook and assignment settings that is why we decided to escalate the case for further review.

INC number: INC0492379

Opened: 2024-09-06 21:22:32

Resolved: 2024-09-09 13:19:49

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Closed

FAD Reason: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

Name of agent: Michael Pan

Team Leader: T3 TL

Team: T3

Category: Mastering - Assignment

Case number: 50558734

INC number: INC0500673

Opened: 2024-09-17 01:49:56

Resolved: 2024-09-17 04:17:09

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Category: Mastering - Gradebook

Questions/Comments/Notes to raise on CTS/Prod Support Call: We understand that this is FAD. This case originated from FS, where the FS team and FS Specialist explained to the EDU that students receive a score of zero due to the settings applied to the assignments, even though they have not completed them yet. Despite this explanation, the EDU insisted that there are some technical issues with the assignments or gradebook. As a result, the FS team decided to escalate the case to TS as the FS Specialist mentioned that they have seen similar case escalated to TS. From the Tier 2 side, we've reviewed the support site before I escalate the case, though I was not able to mention that the EDU needs to uncheck the box each time they manage incompletes and point out that the EDU has the option to delete the zero scores. But we were able to inform the EDU that this is working as designed. We also provided the support site - https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm to the instructor for review; however, the EDU continues to insist that there is something wrong with their gradebook and assignment settings that is why we decided to escalate the case for further review.

Case number: 50416963

INC number: INC0492379

Opened: 2024-09-06 21:22:32

Resolved: 2024-09-09 13:19:49

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Closed

FAD Reason: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

Opened: 2024-09-11 17:59:55

Assignment group: Revel Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD, Scoring_Policy

Assigned to: Jena Subrat

Resolution notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

Name of agent: Rica Aiza Cruz

Team Leader: Ronald Villa

Team: T2

Category: XL - Gradebook

Case number: 50195850

INC number: INC0475294

Opened: 2024-08-21 10:49:53

Resolved: 2024-08-21 12:56:40

Assignment group: 3PL Product Escalation

Tags: 3PL_1.3, 3PL_FAD, 3PL_GS

Assigned to: Ben Lethlean

Resolution notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Name of agent: Christopher Bustamante

Team Leader: Frezalin Bascara

Team: T2

Category: Mastering - Gradebook

Questions/Comments/Notes to raise on CTS/Prod Support Call: We understand that this is FAD. This case originated from FS, where the FS team and FS Specialist explained to the EDU that students receive a score of zero due to the settings applied to the assignments, even though they have not completed them yet. Despite this explanation, the EDU insisted that there are some technical issues with the assignments or gradebook. As a result, the FS team decided to escalate the case to TS as the FS Specialist mentioned that they have seen similar case escalated to TS. From the Tier 2 side, we've reviewed the support site before I escalate the case, though I was not able to mention that the EDU needs to uncheck the box each time they manage incompletes and point out that the EDU has the option to delete the zero scores. But we were able to inform the EDU that this is working as designed. We also provided the support site - https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm to the instructor for review; however, the EDU continues to insist that there is something wrong with their gradebook and assignment settings that is why we decided to escalate the case for further review.

Case number: 50416963

INC number: INC0492379

Opened: 2024-09-06 21:22:32

Resolved: 2024-09-09 13:19:49

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Closed

FAD Reason: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Once the graded items flow to the ISS > Grade Sync area, and the applicable items have been marked for sync and they read "Enabled", those will then appear in the D2L gradebook. Please reopen if this does not resolve the grade sync issues. Omit Results items are found in the MyLab Gradebook > Change Weights area...

MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

Name of agent: Michael Pan

Team Leader: T3 TL

Team: T3

Category: Mastering - Assignment

Case number: 50558734

INC number: INC0500673

Opened: 2024-09-17 01:49:56

Resolved: 2024-09-17 04:17:09

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Name of agent: Christopher Bustamante

Team Leader: Frezalin Bascara

Team: T2

Category: Mastering - Gradebook

Questions/Comments/Notes to raise on CTS/Prod Support Call: We understand that this is FAD. This case originated from FS, where the FS team and FS Specialist explained to the EDU that students receive a score of zero due to the settings applied to the assignments, even though they have not completed them yet. Despite this explanation, the EDU insisted that there are some technical issues with the assignments or gradebook. As a result, the FS team decided to escalate the case to TS as the FS Specialist mentioned that they have seen similar case escalated to TS. From the Tier 2 side, we've reviewed the support site before I escalate the case, though I was not able to mention that the EDU needs to uncheck the box each time they manage incompletes and point out that the EDU has the option to delete the zero scores. But we were able to inform the EDU that this is working as designed. We also provided the support site - https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm to the instructor for review; however, the EDU continues to insist that there is something wrong with their gradebook and assignment settings that is why we decided to escalate the case for further review.

Case number: 50416963

INC number: INC0492379

Opened: 2024-09-06 21:22:32

Resolved: 2024-09-09 13:19:49

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Closed

FAD Reason: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

INC number: INC0495929

Opened: 2024-09-11 17:59:55

Assignment group: Revel Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD, Scoring_Policy

Assigned to: Jena Subrat

Resolution notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. Changing the Global Scoring policy only makes changes to items that have not been engaged by a student and locked. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

Name of agent: Rica Aiza Cruz

Team Leader: Ronald Villa

Team: T2

Category: XL - Gradebook

Case number: 50195850

INC number: INC0475294

Opened: 2024-08-21 10:49:53

Resolved: 2024-08-21 12:56:40

Assignment group: 3PL Product Escalation

Tags: 3PL_1.3, 3PL_FAD, 3PL_GS

Assigned to: Ben Lethlean

Resolution notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

Name of agent: Michael Pan

Team Leader: T3 TL

Team: T3

Category: Mastering - Assignment

Case number: 50558734

INC number: INC0500673

Opened: 2024-09-17 01:49:56

Resolved: 2024-09-17 04:17:09

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

If, however, you select unlimited tries for assessments with questions that have a set number of answers, Revel limits the tries to the number of answers minus 1, as described above.

Mastering Biology - Student Late Penalty

Agent: Veronica Cavara

Case number: 50723660

INC number: INC0518679

Opened: 2024-10-04 06:03:08

Resolved: 2024-10-04 23:22:20

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: incorrect_score, MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: This is expected behavior in Mastering Platform Update. The original due date for the assignment was September 24th; however, the instructor applied individual student settings to the assignment (I suspect after the student completed it) to give this student a due date October 3rd. Unlike legacy Mastering, Mastering Platform Update does not automatically regrade student submissions when a new due date is applied. For the new settings to apply to the student's submission, the student needs to reopen the assignment. Since the new due date has passed, the instructor will need to push it out to any time in the future, and then the student will need to reopen and save the assignment before the new due date passes.

Name of agent: Christopher Bustamante

Team Leader: Frezalin Bascara

Team: T2

Category: MMND - Gradebook

Questions/Comments/Notes to raise on CTS/Prod Support Call: We understand that this is FAD. This case originated from FS, where the FS team and FS Specialist explained to the EDU that students receive a score of zero due to the settings applied to the assignments, even though they have not completed them yet. Despite this explanation, the EDU insisted that there are some technical issues with the assignments or gradebook. As a result, the FS team decided to escalate the case to TS as the FS Specialist mentioned that they have seen similar case escalated to TS. From the Tier 2 side, we've reviewed the support site before I escalate the case, though I was not able to mention that the EDU needs to uncheck the box each time they manage incompletes and point out that the EDU has the option to delete the zero scores. But we were able to inform the EDU that this is working as designed. We also provided the support site - https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm to the instructor for review; however, the EDU continues to insist that there is something wrong with their gradebook and assignment settings that is why we decided to escalate the case for further review.

Case number: 50416963

INC number: INC0492379

Opened: 2024-09-06 21:22:32

Resolved: 2024-09-09 13:19:49

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Closed

FAD Reason.: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

Assigned to: Ben Lethlean

Resolution notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

Name of agent: Michael Pan

Team Leader: T3 TL

Team: T3

Case number: 50558734

INC number: INC0500673

Opened: 2024-09-17 01:49:56

Resolved: 2024-09-17 04:17:09

Assignment group: Mastering Product Escalations

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Assigned to: Tana Regan

Resolution notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.
